9  
The Offering of Life  

The path of our faith is a path that replaces the life of offerings, and everyone knows this. This offering came to be because, as you all know, it arose from the fall. After Adam fell, he could not stand on God's side nor on Satan's side, being in a middle position. Therefore, he took the place of Adam and separated Cain and Abel. Although Cain and Abel were separated, they are still in a position where God cannot claim them as His own. Because of this, whether one offers the offering properly or not determines whether one stands on the side of heaven or not, as you have learned through the principles. You have learned that an offering is a conditional object to determine ownership on either God's side or Satan's side.  
   
Human beings, who have fallen, must approach God through offerings. Thus, we must clearly understand that without establishing the substantial reality of offerings that God can always own, from individuals to families, tribes, nations, and the world, the heavenly mission and the nation that God can govern cannot emerge.  

Originally, offerings are to be placed on the altar and split apart. If the altar symbolizes a sanctified land, then the divided items symbolize distinguished objects.  
   
Now, the shedding of blood, the act of splitting and shedding blood, signifies the condition for indemnity, in other words, it means to sanctify, to remove Satan's blood, and to completely settle Satan's subjective conditions.  
   
In this light, during the Old Testament era, offerings were made through material things, and thus animals and all other items had to be sanctified. They had to be sanctified in heart and externally as well. They must be sanctified both inside and out.  
   
Therefore, when there is an altar, we must ascend there instead of the altar. Offering is not for God, but for ourselves. We must understand that it is offered for humanity. This cumbersome task of establishing such conditions for indemnity arose due to the fall.  
   
Thus, this is not for God; it burdens God. You must understand that by offering this offering, I draw closer to God. Whether God accepts the offering or not means that it is merely acknowledging and permitting it. Since you are carrying out the providence of restoration through the process of offerings, who must make the pledge to return to the original position of a person who is completely one with the offering and distinguished from Satan? It is not God who does it, but I must do it.  
   
Until now, all acts of offering in religious ceremonies have developed from ancient superstitious religions to the present. It has always been centered around this object of offering, thinking that the deity likes offerings. Ultimately, it must be understood that it is for myself, for humanity. Therefore, among the offerings made for humanity, there are offerings that represent individual humans, familial humans, tribal humans, national humans, and global humans.

Humans must unite with God through offerings  

From this perspective, we must recognize that God cannot continue the history of offerings forever. We must see the end of the history of offerings. He needs people who can become one with him, taking the Jewish church or the nation of Israel as the altar to become the offering. The Messiah came because of people, not the other way around.

The Ownership of God and Humanity

We humans have desires. As long as we have desires, we will certainly center ourselves and seek to establish all relationships. 

Human beings are beings that can dominate the concept of ownership. If there are good and bad things in this world, our universal desire is to eliminate the bad and make all the good things our own. This is a desire that is common to any individual, family, nation, or any group with a certain ideology or thought. We know that humanity has developed from the individual era to the tribal, national, and world eras based on such desires.

Looking at the world now, there are two concepts of ownership. There is a democratic world that emphasizes personal ownership, and there is communism that emphasizes ownership from a holistic, national perspective. In this view, religion is included in the democratic world that emphasizes individualism. In the communist system that emphasizes national ownership, there is no religion at all. The concept of God is completely absent.

Therefore, in a communist national system, the concept of ownership cannot be emphasized beyond the national standard.

In our democratic world, personal ownership is emphasized, and this is interconnected, and we can glimpse that the concept of God can intervene in that ownership concept.

This is what is currently clashing. And looking at the present, we can see that the individualistic democratic world system is entering a stage of collapse. The communist world is also trying to connect as a global system based on such national concepts of ownership, but we see that it is also currently in a state of division.

In this light, before we can make the world our own, we must think about whose ownership humanity is. Who is trying to own it? It is because people are trying to own it that we must ask, who exactly are these people? Furthermore, on what basis and from what standpoint are those who claim ownership trying to do so? This is the problem.

Will people become the world's, or will the world become theirs?
What do you think? "The world belongs to humanity." Undoubtedly, the world must be owned by humans. The perspective that prioritizes human dignity in ownership is a secondary position. Individual desires are necessary because there are people, and the desires of nations or ethnic groups are also necessary because there are people; without people, all of this is unnecessary. Therefore, it is undeniable that humans must be in a position of superiority where they can dominate the concept of ownership and always have control over the things they wish to own, or over this world.

The concept of ownership centered around communism and democracy
Now, when we consider communism in the context of a communist world, we must ask whether human value is fully recognized within the framework of the state. In other words, does the concept of state ownership include humans, or does the concept of ownership exist within the framework of human rights centered around humans? We cannot ignore this question. From this perspective, communism centers around the party, which is considered absolute. "Everything must absolutely obey the party's commands and must remain eternally within its jurisdiction," and thus, "the world must be made communist."

Then, where is the value of humanity that communism claims to uphold? It is said that human value exists in absolute obedience to the party. It is inverted. Individuals must sacrifice themselves and everything for the party. So, is the party eternal? What kind of eternal rights does it possess? This is in a state of flux. Communism is evolving. If it were an absolute and eternal standard, there might be some official definition or truth system in absolute obedience and absolute compliance, but there cannot be such a thing when it comes to change.

People living within this framework will always yearn for human sovereignty, human rights, and a new, free worldview centered around humanity. As you all know, Germany is divided by barriers between East and West, and if these barriers were removed, all East Germans would cross over to West Germany. They would all come over. Why is that? Because human rights are being violated, leading to this automatic outcome. If there were a free system that defended human rights within the framework of this communist regime, it could completely conquer the world and more. From this perspective, we can conclude that communism is destined to clash with a new concept of human rights and property rights in the human world, leading to a confrontation and eventual overthrow.

Now, looking at the democratic world, democracy is positioned in individualism, while at the same time, it has a totalitarian aspect centered around religion. Religion is anchored in the concept of God. God is the center of the whole. Because God is the center of the whole, there is a way for the entirety to communicate under God's name.

The offerings you give to the church are meant to connect with the whole. What would happen if there were no religion in this democratic world? All individualistic pursuits would inevitably hit a wall. There, individualism is always imposed, and conflicts are always ongoing. Frequent conflicts arise. Hasn't religion been the one to harmonize this in the democratic world until now? Peace, freedom, and philanthropy do not exist in individualism. Are such things present for individuals? When the concept of ownership is strong around freedom, such things cannot exist.

If the U.S. were to abandon all collectivism and choose individualism, it would fail.
So, what kind of country is the United States? The U.S. is a state system centered around individualistic ownership. In this context, if the U.S. emerged from individualistic ideas and cooperated with the world in the 1960s, where did that idea come from? "We must cooperate with the world, the world must become one, we must create a UN organization, and the world must be seen as one family." Where did that concept come from?

It can be said that the U.S. did this to dominate the world, for the sake of America. It can also be seen that the U.S. did this because of God's will, to create one world. Thus, we can speak of these two perspectives.

Then, which one is correct? Some people see it as all incorrect. Why? If it was done for America, it retreated without going to the end. If it was for God's will, it should have fulfilled God's will, but it retreated without doing so. This leads to the conclusion that both God and America are wrong. 

Therefore, one could argue that democracy and the worldview centered around religion are all incorrect.

Considering this, think about how much damage has been caused to the world by America's attempt to dominate and support the democratic world. If, immediately after World War II, everyone had said they did not understand the world and had taken a position like today's America, then today, Korea, Vietnam, and the entire world would not have suffered under communism and would not have transitioned to communism. At that time, the world, particularly the Asian region, was moving toward communism without conflict, and many lives would not have been sacrificed. However, due to America's support, how much material and human loss occurred?

Because of this, even communists say, "Let's take down this America," and even those who are not communists say, "Damn America." Both have become enemies. As a result, even countries that were part of the democratic world have come to say, "We trusted this America..." and have transitioned to supporting communism, saying, "Let's take down America through communism." This has led to such outcomes.

Ultimately, who has come to fight against America? It is not just communists but also those who were once part of the democratic world. This is the world that has been created. It is currently turning in this direction. In front of America, what is more frightening than communism is that those who were part of the democratic world are more outraged because America has failed to take responsibility and has abandoned them. This is a fact we must recognize. Americans must understand this. If that is the case...

When we look at America as a country, it encompasses all these nations. Americans are a composite nation. If all these nations within America connect with their respective ethnic groups and engage in movements, will this become a movement to help America or a movement to destroy America? "To destroy..." If there is a possibility that communism can unify the world with some ideology or claim, then there will be cooperation in that direction.

From this perspective, if it is true that America sought to embrace the whole world immediately after World War II, and if that was for the sake of the American entity, then all policies of America for the sake of the American entity are failures. If God initiated this, then God also fails. If God did this, God cannot fail, so why did it result in failure? If America does not go as God desires, it can lead to failure. That conclusion is valid. If America acted as God wanted, then America cannot fail; neither can God fail, and this logic is established here.

Goodness exists within the totalitarianism centered on God.

Think about it. Did communism create itself? It is permitted by God. We must understand that the entire world must belong to totalitarianism. We must belong to totalitarianism centered around God. God has taught that totalitarianism centered around Him must exist eternally. The entire world exists under God. The model of totalitarianism is that it must be governed under God. When that happens, both God and humanity agree.

Who is God? He is the ancestor of humanity, the Father. Therefore, what God desires is automatically what humanity desires. Thus, individuals can exist within the domain centered around the whole. While America can exist to save the entire world, it cannot exist in a way that disregards the entire world. This is God's perspective. However, America is trying to rise above God. It claims to act according to its own will. But that cannot be the case.

Therefore, totalitarianism centered around God is recognized. When ownership of the entire world is determined centered on God and humanity, we can conclude that this is idealism. Does that seem plausible? "Yes."

Then, what do goodness and religion desire? What are they trying to achieve? What does religion want to do, and what does goodness want to achieve? What do they want to gain through goodness, and what do they want to gain through true religion? We must understand that all systems, whether great or small, are distinguished based on conditions that can help achieve an absolute world.

Does goodness impose individualism? "No." When someone says a person is good, do they mean that person acts entirely for themselves? "No." Within the conditions that serve the whole, the range of what one can possess and occupy determines higher dignity and more valuable existence. Isn't that so? Why is that? It is because they are connected with God, are with God, and belong to God. We must understand that.

All ideologies pursuing goodness belong to totalitarianism. Within the totalitarianism centered around God... We can find this concept here. Thus, great religions are universal. They transcend nations. The ownership of that religion transcends states; it is established in a way that states cannot interfere.

So, what does God want to achieve through religion? Would He leave failing religions as they are and call that goodness? Happy Unification Church

A happy person is someone who has something to give and receive.

So, why has such a person become that way? The problem is simple. They do not have the object they can give freely, nor do they have the object they can receive freely. Therefore, it concludes that such a place is an unhappy place.

Speaking of women, why are women unhappy? When they cannot give what they want to give and cannot receive what they want to receive, that is when they are unhappy. When there is no object to give to, no matter how precious something they have, they cannot become a happy person, and we can feel this in our daily lives. Even if I have the best diamond in the world, while I have it, it may seem good, but if there is no object to whom I can show it or someone who can enjoy it, no matter how good it is… I always think about that object.

A person with sore eyes is unhappy. A person who cannot see is unhappy. They need to be in a position to give and receive with an object, but the function of that object has been lost. Also, a hungry person is a pitiful person. They cannot receive rice, and… that connection has been cut off. Does that seem right? "Yes."

What is unhappiness? It is when you cannot give what you want to give and cannot receive what you want to receive. The conditions of unhappiness will vary according to that degree. Think about it. Everything is like that.

Living to Love

In that light, what is the most precious thing in a person? It is love, but the word love itself cannot be said alone. Love manifests in complete unity. Because of love, inside and outside become one. Inside and outside become one, and the subject and object become one. After becoming one, they become the same. Women are small, men are big, and their shapes are different. Men have beards like this, and women are smooth; men have thick hands, and women have slender ones…

Because of love, they can be equal, and in terms of value, they can become the same, and in terms of weight, they can also be the same, but if you take love away, they cannot be the same. "Yes," the word "muni" is connected to "discuss" and "discussion." What it means is that "muni" (問議) refers to a conversation between unequal parties. It signifies a discussion between someone of a higher status and someone of a lower status. Even among equals, it involves people of different ranks coming together to discuss. When a lower person seeks to consult a higher person, that is referred to as "muni." In essence, it aligns perfectly with the idea of 'let's discuss between us, the lowly humans, and God.' Our Pride

Everyone wants to boast about everything centered around themselves. That is human nature. 

What God and humans want to boast about

You want to boast about your own body, about your partner, and about your children. You all know this well. This is the same for both Eastern and Western people. Also, it is the same for people of the past, present, and future, and for both the talented and the untalented. It is the same for both the wicked and the good. Isn’t that right? "Yes."

Then, if there is a God, an absolute God, what would that God want to boast about? God is the same. So, what does God want to boast about? God would want to boast about Himself. Also, He would want to boast about what He possesses. 

Then, He would want to boast about the object of His love. 

When you look at it this way, it doesn’t come down to many things. He would want to boast about what He has, whether He created it or acquired it in some way. Then He would want to boast about Himself and about the object of His love. There is nothing else. Think about it; what else could there be? Isn’t it the same for us humans? You want to boast about what you have. You also want to boast about yourself and about your object of love.

This is true for individuals, and since individuals are like that, God is like that too. And since God is like that, my individual self is the same. Also, my individual self is the same for my family.

Pride of the United States

Next, as a nation… You sing songs boasting about America. There are many songs praising America. There are songs that boast about it. You boast about the American flag, the Stars and Stripes, as a symbol of the nation, right? But if you think about it quietly, it’s nothing at all. There are 50 stars symbolizing the 50 states, and there are 13 stripes. Red stripes, blue stripes… It’s simple.

Why are there thirteen stripes? They say that the thirteen stripes represent the thirteen colonies that became the United States, but I don’t think so. I think that if the thirteen stripes on the American flag represent Jesus and the twelve disciples combined, that would be much cooler. No one thinks like that. So, which is better? "I like the teacher’s idea better." 

Then it becomes, "Wow, America is a global nation, a nation that has the potential to unify the world." And what about the 50 stars? If we say, "The 50 stars represent the 50 nations of the world," how wonderful would that be? Then you would say, "Oh, America is a truly great country." But no one thinks about that. 

Now, when explaining the American flag, if we attach what Reverend Moon said, wouldn’t America become a country that can develop significantly in the future? On that day, we would have to incorporate Reverend Moon’s ideology. You can think like that.

Also, if we think that the 50 states represent 50 nations, and that "the 50 nations are developing towards 70 nations, and that is developing towards 120 nations," how wonderful is that? Why is that? Because centered on Jesus and the twelve disciples, there are 70 disciples and 120 disciples, and if America is undoubtedly a representative nation to expand that meaning globally, how wonderful is that? "In order for that to become one, America is all united. Therefore, it is the model of an ideal Christian nation." That fits perfectly.

But America wants to boast about itself. Do you want to boast? What do you want to boast about? You want to boast about America itself. That is the same as wanting to boast about the individual itself. You want to boast about America itself, the country called America.

What else do you want to boast about? You want to boast about what America has. It’s the same. You want to boast about having economic power. Then you want to boast about democracy, boast about various past achievements, and boast about everything you have. And if someone tries to reject what you want to boast about, you don’t like it.

Then, what else do you want to boast about? You want to boast about the American people, the citizens of America. Isn’t that right?

It is the same for God. What will the ideal world be like in the future? It will be the same. The world is like that, and God’s ideal world is the same. The ideal world boasts about itself. When it says, "The ideal world is like this and that," it boasts. Then it boasts about what the ideal world has. It boasts about the people of the ideal world. Isn’t that so? Isn’t it?

The nature of humans to cover flaws and boast about good things

Some people boast about wearing glasses. Wearing glasses is nothing to boast about. But they walk around saying, "These are gold-rimmed glasses."

Ladies, why do you wear earrings? I think it started because people with ugly ears began to wear them. I don’t think it started because people with beautiful ears wore them. If your ears were beautiful, you would want to boast about them as they are. But because they are ugly, it is a condition to hide the ugly ones.

The same goes for necklaces. Necklaces are the same. People with beautiful necks don’t wear necklaces. I thought about why necklaces became popular in the West. What kind of neck is considered ugly? It’s those with long necks. (Laughter) Therefore, by wearing this, various harmonies are created. When people see it, they don’t think about the long neck; they only look at that, so it gets hidden. (Laughter)

Rings must have started with people who had some ugly flaw on their hands. Isn’t that so? Think about it. That’s how the reasoning connects. Nose rings… You know, I was surprised to see nose rings… (Laughter)

So, what is all of this? All decorations and makeup are to cover all of one’s flaws and reveal beauty. So that’s how it is. Are you all like that? Raise your hand if you’re not like that. Not a single person.

Then how were people in the past? It was the same. People today are the same. Then what about people in the future? The conclusion that they are the same cannot be changed by anyone.

When you look at America, Westerners decorate their restrooms well. Isn’t that so? Why is that? It’s all to cover up and to boast. (Laughter)

So, what about God? What do you think God would be like? God is the same. God is like humans. And in the spirit world… It’s the same while we are alive, and it’s the same after we die. Spirits are the same.

What will you boast about in the spirit world?

So, what will you boast about in the spirit world? Think about it. What do you want to boast about? What will you boast about? You should boast about yourself, but if you want to boast about yourself, there is nothing. There is nothing to boast about. If everything is not close to the standard, there is nothing to boast about. If it is not close to perfection, isn’t there nothing to boast about?

Then, what must happen to boast? Does it have to be fake or real? "Truth." Then what does truth mean? Does it mean I become the standard? It follows the true, unchanging standard. Isn’t there such a thing? Isn’t that right?

If it’s a diamond, it serves as a standard for hardness, and if it’s gold, it serves as a standard for the yellow color, the unchanging light. Pearls are centered around harmony and serve as a standard.

So, if I have gold, I say, "This is real." If you have gold, you also boast that it is real, right? It’s the same. In the spirit world, what will you have to boast about? The conclusion is that you cannot boast without having something that can match the standard of perfection. Is that right or not?

Then what is that standard? Am I the standard? If it’s a standard, it must be God. "Oh, that looks like God." You must be able to say that; you must resemble God to be able to boast. Isn’t that so? "Yes."

The standard of perfection is God.

Everyone, what do you think God’s eyes look like? Does He have one eye or two? "Two." Why? Why does He have two eyes? (Laughter) Huh? Because I can love with two eyes… God loves deeply, so to love me, He must have two eyes. Because I love two eyes… Since I love two eyes, God cannot love me without having two eyes. Because I love with two eyes… To love that person, He must resemble having two eyes.

It’s the same in reverse. Because God has two eyes and loves deeply, those who receive God’s love dislike having one eye or three eyes. Therefore, those who receive God’s love cannot be without two eyes. The beings that can receive that love are us humans, so we cannot be without two eyes. Why? Because to receive God’s love… God dislikes one-eyed and three-eyed beings. So it must be two. Do you understand?

Then what about God’s nose? It resembles me. It’s the same theory. How many mouths does He have? How many mouths? "One." Then how many does God have? "One." What about God’s ears? What about His hands? They are all the same. Why are they the same? Because He likes what resembles Him; He likes things that are the same.

Now, when you look at parents with sons and daughters, who do they love more? Even if the mother and father are not good-looking, they love their children who resemble them more. (Laughter) Is that so? "Yes." Why is it "yes"? Why not "no"? It’s because they resemble them.

When you take a picture, think about it; if an ugly person sits in a beauty pageant photo, when the ugly person comes to get the picture, will they look at their face first or the beautiful people? (Laughter) Answer me. "They look at themselves first." That’s for sure? "Yes." You all resemble me. That’s for sure.

So, the fact that parents love children who resemble them is an undeniable fact when you dig into all the psychological roots. There is no application for the word "no" there.

When baby elephants see, sometimes they stick their noses out of the muddy water and play. If there are babies, they do the same. Even in that water, the mother says she likes her babies. Why? Because they resemble her. It means that whatever resembles you is loved at all times.

Loving people… Can love only happen in a palace? "No." Can’t you love while working in muddy water like the elephant I mentioned earlier? Yesterday, we caught fish in Barrytown, and even in that muddy water, smiling while catching fish, isn’t that love? To boast, it must be centered around God.

Then whose nose does it resemble? It resembles God. Whether it’s small, long, or short, it resembles God. It surely stretches out in the middle, and the shapes are the same, meaning that here is wide and here is narrow; they all resemble each other.

The Desire of All Things

Today, as you all know, is the 15th 'Day of All Things.' Today, I want to briefly talk to you about 'the desire of all things,' that is, what all things desire. 

God created the created world to see the completion of love. The created world was created to fulfill God's purpose. When we say all things, we must think that it includes not only all creatures but everything; all creation is included. That is, it includes people as well. 

Now, when we look at it this way, what is the completion of the purpose of creation? It is the fulfillment of God's will. What is the fulfillment of God's will? It is the completion of God's love. Therefore, ultimately, why did God create the created world? It was not to see people, nor to see all things. Ultimately, it is to see love that can fulfill God's will, and we must clearly understand this. Ultimately, even if God exists... if God exists without love, there is no reason for Him to exist. Because He is the true God, He is also seeking love; He is seeking true love.

Now, then, everyone, we are to become true people. We want to become true people. But what do we do as true people? What kind of person is a true person? A true person is one who receives true love from God. 

Then, how can all created beings exist in the heavenly kingdom on earth, as holy beings? They want to be governed by the love of a true person who receives true love from God. The desire of all created beings is to go to a place where they can be governed by such a person. Ultimately, all creation is looking to go to a place where they can fulfill God's will and the will of humanity through true love. We must understand this fact here.

The Messiah who must complete the love that could not be completed due to the Fall

Everyone, today, God's will has not been fulfilled due to the Fall, and therefore God's completion has not been achieved. God has not completed it. What has not been completed? In love. We must understand that humans, of course, and all things have not reached the position of completion. In love, they have been insufficient. 

Now, having created all things and having created people, because people fell, God became lonely. What should He focus on to love? He cannot love alone. He wanted to love people as His sons and daughters, but He could not achieve it, so He could not see the fulfillment of His will... We must understand that when we say God has not seen the fulfillment, it is in relation to love.

Now, in that sense, what about people? People are the same. Is the love that humans are loving today the completed love, the love that fulfills God's will? We must understand that it is not; they are loving a love that deviates from God's will.

No matter how much parents love their children, no matter how great that love is on this earth today, you must understand that they cannot stand before God. No matter how much love there is between husband and wife, that love cannot stand before God because it is not within the realm of completed love that fulfills God's will. The same goes for love between siblings, or love between a king and his subjects. We know that everything is within the realm of incomplete love. All creation is the same.

So, what has God been doing until now? What has He been doing? He has been trying to find people again. He has been raising a movement to find people from individuals... Since people are spread globally, the historical foundation for developing a global movement is religion.

Thus, God is seeking to find a true woman through the historical process, someone who can truly love. One man must be found to find one woman, according to the principle. That is the idea of the Messiah. That person is the Messiah.

Then, what is the main purpose of that Savior? It is to liberate the incomplete realm of love. We must understand that this is the mission of the Messiah. Because humanity fell and was drawn into the world of Satan, we must find it again. We must receive salvation and be recognized by God, but what will we do with that? We must open a path to reach the position of completed love. The representative for that is the Messiah, that is, the Savior. It is not about finding love in the world of Satan; it is about finding people. If we were to find love, it would mean that there is completed love in the world of Satan. Therefore, unless we rise above the love of the world of Satan, there is no way to connect to heavenly love.

So, what is the responsibility we humans have now? We must overcome the standard of love in the world of Satan by any means necessary. Once we overcome it, from there, we will be drawn into God's completed love. That is the mission of the Messiah. The mission of the Messiah is to lift us up from here.

From this perspective, can God come down to the world of Satan and truly love the people of the world of Satan? He cannot love them. If He could, there would have been no need for the long historical period until now. He would have already saved everyone.

To believe in a religion means to seek salvation, and to seek salvation means to go to the position of completion. Therefore, what does a religious person think? They think that they will love their religious leader and God more than any love in the world of Satan. After making such a vow, they must understand that this is the path of religion. They must go to a love that is greater than worldly love. That is the path that a religious person must take. They must overcome the world of Satan. Therefore, God's love starts from a position above the world of Satan.

Anyone who enters the Unification Church must go through the 7-year course.

So, in the Bible, Jesus said, 'Love me more than anyone else.' This means that unless you love yourself more than your mother, or your sons and daughters, or your spouse, or anyone else, you cannot become a son or daughter of the Father. Why is that? It is because you must emerge from the love of the world of Satan to start from there, and you must enter heaven with the connection of the love of the Messiah. This is an unavoidable principled condition, and we must understand that this is why such words were necessary.

If you are a man, you must go out to the standard of completion following the Messiah. Because you fell at the level of growth, there is a foundation to go to the standard of completion, and there is also a foundation for women to go. So, because there is such a principled foundation, the principle that everyone must go through the 7-year course in the Unification Church comes from here. The 7-year course comes from here.

But why does the Unification Church receive blessings after only 3 years? That is the question. It is because the teacher has already paved the way; because he has paved the way, it is possible. You should think that after your 3 years combined with the teacher's 3 years, it totals 6 years, and then you add one more year to make it 7 years. 

Therefore, the teacher has gone through the 3-year course personally, the 3-year course in the family, the 3-year course in the tribe, the nation, and the world. So, you must lay the foundation and take responsibility to create one.

You must receive blessings and then go through the remaining 3-year course. You must become one. What does that mean? It means that when Adam and Eve fell, they fell at the level of growth, so you must establish the conditions to rise from here. Therefore, you must receive blessings and have children after 3 years. You must understand this. Do you understand what I mean? 

So, the 36 families, 72 families, 120 families, and 430 families have all gone according to this principle. For the people after that, for the 74 couples this time, they were told to go for a period of 7 months to establish conditions to live together. Because they have established such global standards, such things are possible.

Now, when we look at it this way, what has been the purpose of believing in religion until now? It is to meet the Messiah and complete God's love. It is to fulfill the purpose of God's love. Then, you who have entered our Unification Church... There are many people who think that it would be better if I kept my words short when going out to sell newspapers. Why is that? Selling newspapers is to lay a bridge to find a good partner. This is the path to finding a partner. Ultimately, what you are doing by selling newspapers is clearing the obstacles for the love partner to come. 

So, by paving the way for the future bride to follow, the bride can easily come because the man opens the way. This is the activity we must do in the course of the 7-year course.

Then, how does such a statement become principled? Originally, when Adam devotes himself to God, Eve will naturally follow, and when Eve devotes herself and comes before Adam, Adam can also follow her easily. That logic must be established. This is the principle. 

Now, what is the Fall? The Fall is when you put God aside and diligently follow another path. It is the opposite. Do you understand?

Therefore, Abel must teach Cain how to be blessed. That is why I work to pave the way for the one who can be my husband, and I work to pave the way for the one who can be my wife. Therefore, even if the world of Satan opposes and there are difficulties, I must not become like fallen Eve or Adam, and I must overcome it without hesitation, with the conviction that I will step over the Satan who caused the Fall of Adam and Eve. I must have the conviction that no matter what field of the world opposes, I will overcome it without any problems. 

Right now, the stage of Satan is unfolding on a personal, family, tribal, national, and global level. 

Any true religion must overcome this global realm of Satan, which is why Satan will inevitably attack. Therefore, it is a principle that religion will be persecuted.

From that perspective, if a religion is earnestly trying to walk that path centered on the name of God, and if it faces opposition worldwide, the end is near. Through that religion, which is opposed globally, there is a path to unite with the Messiah.

Now, what kind of religion has faced such opposition in history? The Unification Church is that religion. Reverend Moon is opposed in dozens of countries and before all humanity while he is alive. That is different. The Unification Church is different. He is alive and facing opposition from dozens and hundreds of countries. You are being persecuted here.
To be strongly united means that the fact that those who persecute cannot lead us away has become a condition that can surpass global persecution. That is why the foundation of God's will is established here. Do you understand? 
“Yes”

Why is that? Why, why is this? It is to seek God's love. To seek God's love, Cain and Abel must become one according to our principle of restoration through indemnity. Cain and Abel are enemies. They should not become one like this. If they become one like this, the distance becomes the same. (While writing on the board) One side is opposite. This is like this, and this is like this; the way to heaven and the world of Satan is opposite. It is becoming one in opposition. If this crosses over, everything becomes heavenly. If it is drawn over, everything becomes heavenly. 

So, Abel must teach Cain how to submit. He must teach him. Abel must teach Cain how to submit. Then he will win. Here, members of the Unification Church think about the Cain and Abel issue, “Ah, Cain must originally submit before Abel,” but that is not true. If you do not clearly understand this principle, it will be a big problem. They teach that “originally, Cain must go this way,” and after teaching that, when they take on that role, they must rise to a position where they can take the lead. Then what is the center? It must be taught with love. You must love Cain more than anyone else. When you realize that you love him more than anyone else, Cain will turn around. You draw him in with the compass of love. With the compass of love. 

Our Unification Church members, although they may not know, I see that everyone likes the teacher. Is that right? “Yes.” But I do not believe that. “No.” Although I do not believe it, when viewed from the perspective of principles, it must be that way; because I am trying to go by principles, such phenomena must occur. 

Yesterday, when I met the Korean Folk Ballet and asked if they wanted to return to Japan, they said they did not want to go. When I asked why, they said it was because the teacher is in America. Hearing that, I thought that all Japanese people tend to say things to please others. (Laughter) What do you think? Is that why? Why is that? You all should answer. It must be that way. It must be that way. Otherwise, I think the most pitiful person in the world is Reverend Moon. 

I sometimes hear from my mother. She says, “That person just wants to go out as soon as he opens his eyes. He wants to go out and wander around.” Why is that? If I rest at home, it is comfortable, right? When I am tired, I can take a nap, and when it is lunchtime, they will bring me food, and if I ask, they will do as I say, so why wander around, suffering? Today, in fact, it is also tiring. However, I do it because I know that through this, the path for Unification Church members becomes easier, and the way for the spiritual world and the Unification Church to become one becomes easier. 

What principle is behind that? If you are in the position of a parent, there are children, and since the foundation laid by the parents is inherited by the children, the principle of inheritance in the parent-child relationship is that if the parents work hard, the children work less. Do you understand what I mean? “Yes.” 

Even though the teacher has suffered throughout his life, going in and out of prison, he never thought, “Oh, I can’t live. I can’t go.” He thought, “In the future, when my mother is born on this earth, she will not suffer and will walk the path I have paved.” It is the same principle. You are the same. Do you understand what I mean? That is why even in such difficulties, ultimately, the path for your partner to walk… (The recording briefly cuts off) 

That is why the most difficult thing is individual restoration and family restoration. That is the hardest thing. Why is that? When an individual wins, a partner appears, and when a partner appears, a family is formed, and when a family is formed, children are born. Therefore, no matter how much persecution comes from the world, there is a foundation where a wife can comfort me and children can comfort me. When that expands externally, it is like having global children, so Americans support me, and people from around the world support me, and allies are formed. That is why national standards are not harder than individual standards and family standards. Do you understand this principle? 

That is why now, in the Unification Church, all young people like you are coming in. They come in before getting married and suffer to the death. Before getting married, they want to endure all the suffering that exists. Individuals must be filled, families must be filled, and all must oppose. The nation must oppose, and the world must oppose; they must all be pushed in. 

Even in a position where one can say, “I am the only one left,” one must continue to believe and move forward. 

Now, if there is no teacher and no Unification Church and only oneself is being opposed, then there is no teacher, no Unification Church members, and only oneself is in that situation, one will pray, “Am I the only one left in the universe?” When I see the teacher, it seems he is just cursing and sympathizing, and when I see the Unification Church members, they all seem to be biting and trying to make it unbearable; they do not show any sympathy. You must go to that place of “I am the only one left.” After that, it seems that heaven does not recognize you. You feel like you are the only one left in the universe… 

However, if this path is not taken, and if this path is not right, you must believe and move on. If that happens, you will rise to the highest standard of faith globally. Only then can God trust you, and the church can trust you, and everyone can trust you. That is because I made you believe, not because God made you believe. I believed. Therefore, everything that is honored, elevated, and gained through that faith is mine, mine. Do you understand? 

You all feel lonely a lot, right? Do not think of your mother and father whom you loved in the world. If you have someone you loved in the past, do not think of that person. Do not think of your siblings. You must think of God. Even if you die, you must think of God. Even if the whole world betrays you and opposes you, even if I die, I will believe and die! If that happens, what will happen in the spiritual world? I want to know this! Let’s study it once!” And then, you should go and die and see what happens. 

I want to know what happens to me after I die. How does it compare to others, to those who have not died? I am curious about that. If you die like that, the whole spiritual world will mobilize to welcome you. Why? Why is that? It is because of the law of indemnity. Our human ancestors abandoned God because of disbelief, abandoned the angelic world, abandoned all things, abandoned husbands, abandoned wives, and abandoned nations; they abandoned everything. By entering into that place of abandonment and believing in heaven, everything will be found. It is restoration, restoration. Do you understand what I mean? “Yes.” The teacher has walked that path. 

However, you all do not have to do that because the teacher is here. You just have to follow unconditionally. Do you understand what I mean? “Yes.” (Laughter) But the problem is that you do not follow the teacher and say you will go alone. Then you must go this path. After going this path, you must follow the teacher again. There is no other way. 

Everyone wants to meet a partner who has God's love. 

Now, in the world, everyone says do not follow Reverend Moon, and the nation says do not follow him, and everyone opposes. But why do you want to follow Reverend Moon? What does Reverend Moon have? What is the connection? I do not know. It is because my heart is like that, so I cannot help it. I like him; I like him, that is why. Is that true? “Yes.” I do not know. You all probably know better than I do. I think so, but you know better. Why? Because I have lived that way and realized that heaven is with me, so if you do the same, the teacher cannot help but love you, and heaven cannot help but love you. That is the principle. 

Why is that? It is because the path to find a love that does not exist in the world is the original path, so you must understand that your nature cannot help but move that way. 

Then what is the wish of a woman? Let’s quickly conclude what the wish of all things is. So, what is the wish of a woman? “If there is a man who loves me… this is my wish,” she thinks. What kind of love? True love. Then how should true love be expressed? The greatest wish of a woman is to meet a husband who loves on behalf of God, who represents God. 

God is the unique being, the absolute and unchanging being. Therefore, He does not just kill and recreate people because they have fallen. That is absolute. Because He is unique and absolutely unchanging, He says to restore. Therefore, no matter how unworthy a person is, he is the unique, unchanging, and absolute object of God's love. This is God's true love. 

So, what is the wish of a woman? She desires a man who treats her absolutely, uniquely. It is one and only one. After that, it is unchanging. That is why she thinks her partner is an absolute, unique, and unchanging being. She desires such a man. In that position, she wishes for a love that binds her tightly with absolute love, making it impossible for her to fall away. Even if she is pulled by one hair, she wants a man who will be drawn in and cannot be pulled away. This is the wish of a woman. 

I do not know because I am not a woman, but from a principled perspective, I think that the greatest wish of women is to desire a man who has love on behalf of God. Think about it. If there is a person who is absolute, unique, and unchanging, the more you see him, the more he looks like God, the more he looks good, and the more he looks greater than the universe. So, putting God aside, she says, “I do not like God. I like this man.” (Laughter) That is the wish of a woman. Do you understand? 

Then what about men? It is the opposite. It is the same. These dull men, do you understand? “Yes.” (Laughter) That is the love that God desires. 

When united in love, God automatically comes in. 

When these two are united, God automatically comes in there. He will be with them automatically. Then, to whom does God's love manifest? It manifests to me and to my partner. Why must we regard our partner as absolute, unique, and unchanging? It is to pave the way to guide the absolute, unique, and unchanging subject. It is necessary to pave the way to guide such a person. Do you understand what I mean? “Yes.” Therefore, we must have a man and woman who possess completed love, a couple with love, and children with love. 

The parents must provide education that their children can follow. The mother and father must educate. Children also fight. Our children sometimes fight too. Then do you fight like your mother and father? If that happens, that is a problem. It cannot be corrected. If both are fighting, how can it be corrected? “What, if mom and dad are fighting, why is that?” It should not be like that. There will come a time when they realize that fighting brings no benefit. That is it. So, when I see my children fighting, I say, “Fight, fight!” Just like many people in the restoration process get tired of fighting and seek God, when a loser eventually comes out of the fighting, they will surely come back to their parents saying they were wrong for fighting. 

In the future, they will realize that. They will not come crying after fighting, but will come to their parents without fighting and say, “Mom, Dad! This brother is doing this, and my younger sibling is doing that. I want to fight; what should I do?” If they do that, they will receive love. They should report before they fight. Then they will be loved. “Hey, this kid has potential. He is better than his sister and brother.” That is how it will be. It is the same between God and humanity. It is the same between parents and children. Do you understand? The mother and father must become one and become one with the children. They must become one like that. It should not be made one with fists, but with love. You must understand that all things desire to receive love in front of a family equipped with such love. 

That is why all things are longing for God's love, longing for the love of parents, that is, the love of Adam and Eve, and longing for the love of the children who combine the love of God and the love of Adam and Eve. You must understand that they are longing for the love of three generations. In this regard, you must realize that the existence of a son is destined to be loved more than the parents. Because he receives God's love and the love of parents, he is in a position better than Adam and Eve; you must understand that he is the son or daughter of Adam and Eve. That is why the son is a direct line, a vertical line. You must understand that the parent-child relationship is a vertical relationship. 

However, the relationship between husband and wife is a horizontal relationship. Now, why is that? How can we say that? We can understand it with our hearts. When we look at American families, even though they are divorcing, they all say they want to make their children their direct descendants, right? Why is that? It is because they are hopeful beings who can inherit God's love and the love of true parents in the future, so they want to hold onto that. The universe is holding onto that. The spiritual world is also hoping for that. 

The sin of violating true love has no law of forgiveness. 

In the spiritual world, what is the most fearful law? You must understand that there is no law more fearful than the law that governs the sin of putting a child to death. Why is that? It is because it is something that even God could not do. Therefore, there is no law of forgiveness. It cannot be forgiven. The things that God can forgive can be forgiven, but this is something that even God cannot do, so it concludes that even God cannot forgive it. That is why it is the most fearful sin. You must understand that this is something that cannot be tolerated. On the other hand, parents who say they will die for their children are supported by God. He says, “You are like me!” Parents who die for their children can go to heaven. Do you understand? 

You all, in our Unification Church, will you get married and abandon your children and run away, or not? “We will not run away.” If you abandon your children and go to a fun house after getting married, and your children come to you, will you chase them away or welcome them? You must not refuse to welcome them.
Because of that, this law is... As long as the new and strong new ones cannot become the owners of water, there is no value for humans as the owners of water. It means they are worse than animals. Do you understand what I mean? Saying that humans are worse than animals is not about the face or the physique, but it is about love. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." 

So what is the wish of all things? It is to receive God's love and the love of the perfected Adam and Eve, and at the same time, to receive the love of the perfected Adam and Eve's sons and daughters, which combines God's love and parental love. That is the wish of all things. 

That is why what is our most precious inheritance? It is to pass on God's love and the true love of parents to the children, which is the greatest inheritance that does not exist in this world. We must understand this. We must introduce God well. We must understand well what God's love is like. Because we do not know this, we must become parents who can love like God and can replace God as their parents. 

In that sense, if members of our Unification Church commit a crime against their conscience, they must repent before their sons and daughters more than any other sin. This is faster than praying for repentance before God. If the child forgives the parent's sin, God cannot help but forgive as well. Also, when the son forgives the parents when they ask for forgiveness from a position of complete unity with them, God forgives that child's sin as well. 

The only problem is that there is no way to forgive the violation of God's love, true love. We must understand this. Violating true love cannot be forgiven. Why? Because if God forgives that, it means He has not carried out the restoration process until now. To leave an absolute love before the absolute God, it is inevitably impossible to forgive. To create eternal, absolute, unchanging love, it is unavoidable. If that is forgiven, the unique nature is broken. The absolute nature is broken. Everything is broken. The unchanging nature is also broken. Do you understand? 

There is no law to forgive the violation of true love. 

Are there not many such things in American society? Men who break up other people's well-off families, or sins that destroy relationships centered around love cannot be forgiven. They are treated as special cases. In the future, when we men build families, we should not be tempted but should praise when we see true couples living happily and beautiful men and women living joyfully. We should be able to praise, saying, "I want to be like that..." This should be regarded as a precious thing that can be left as a treasure in the universe, like an exhibit in the museum of human families in the universe. 

God wants such families. 

All things also desire true three-fold love. God hopes that what He loves will extend to Adam and Eve, and through Adam and Eve's children, it will reach all things. Adam and Eve want to carry God's love and reach all things through their children. Furthermore, the children of Adam want to carry God's love and the love of their parents and then love all things. 

Then all things want to say, "Hey, I thought all things were the worst, but I have gained the privilege of receiving God's love, Adam and Eve's love, and the love of Adam and Eve's sons and daughters, these three-fold loves." They say, "Because I am such a being, I am God's treasure." They say, "Since I am a being that receives so much love, I must return something holy." Thus, all things become the most loving symbols before us humans and before heaven, and because they can partake in any deep sign of love, they become flesh and become God's flesh, and can realize all the personalities of the spirit world, becoming something of great value. That is the gift of love. That becomes the power of God's love, the power of human love, and the power of the love of Adam's sons and daughters, transforming into a higher dimension of love. 

"Though it seems lowly, through the human body, with the heart and body united, it can reach the invisible, infinite realm of God's love." This is my flesh. The heart is connected to the spirit world. All things can exert influence even to the invisible world of God. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." When viewed this way, how sacred and beautiful is that world? That is the wish of all things, the wish of Adam and Eve's sons, the wish of Adam and Eve, and the wish of God. 

Then, can you men and women have such a heart of love when facing all things? "Yes." What is the "yes"? You complain when you eat, you complain when you wear clothes, saying, "Why was this body born? It would be better to die." How much have you complained? When you walk, try saying, "Oh, earth, I am sorry, I am sorry," and walk gently. If you walk with that heart, your feet will be supported. (Demonstrates with actions) (Applause) 

Even when you relieve yourself in nature, how sorry do you feel? You think it is a pity, but this will become fertilizer... (Recording briefly cuts out) In the desert, it is embarrassing to relieve yourself and look back, but in the forest, if you do it with a loving heart, it connects. (Laughs) 

When we look at what makes a literary work a masterpiece, it is all about cleverly using symbolic phrases. "I am like a bird, like the eyes of a dove, like a butterfly, like water, like a frolicking frog, like a frolicking goldfish..." That is it. Well-crafted literary works are masterpieces. There is nothing else. Isn't that so? "Yes." Why is that? Because they are trying to express their heart of love in nature. It means they are related through the heart of love. But do not think, "Are we humans worse than all things?" Do not think that you are worse than all things. 

The human body contains all things. Look. The heart is like a stem, the stomach is like a root, and the lungs are like leaves. Everything is contained within. The lungs are like tree leaves, and everything is contained. There is nothing in the human body that does not contain all the elements of this earth. Likewise, everything from the heavenly kingdom is contained. Everything from the spirit world is also contained. Therefore, when I, as a person, move, the heavenly kingdom is in turmoil, and the world of all things is in turmoil. Such things happen. 

When living alone, completely settle the path of indemnity. 

That is why my happy time is not just my happiness; all things are happy, and the spirit world is happy. Therefore, people must live happily. To do so, you must understand that there is no way but to live for the sake of others. A person who lives with gratitude will always feel like they are living a heavenly life on this earth. 

Farming is for nature, for animals. You must think that way. When you see nature, you should praise it as highly as God and higher than yourself. That is living for the sake of others. If you live with gratitude, you will feel that you are living a heavenly life on earth. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." 

So when everyone enters the Unification Church, they will have difficult activities, and our restoration process is truly difficult... When living a single life, you must endure much. Then, couples should suffer a little less, and then the sons and daughters should suffer a little, going through these three stages, and it must be clearly understood that the historical indemnity must be completed through the family. 

Why? Because until now, God has struggled for a long time to restore one Adam, to send one Messiah. He has struggled to find just one person, just me. 

When you become a member of the Unification Church, you are told to receive global persecution from the standpoint of one man and one woman. Accept it! Heaven says to receive all persecution. When the two meet, they can love each other more deeply because they know the suffering they have endured. They can find deep love. You must understand this. How much will you love the child born among them? Because you can love deeper than any parent in the world, you can give birth to sons and daughters who can cross over to the heavenly kingdom. By becoming someone who sacrifices everything and then receives blessings to give birth to sons and daughters, you will give birth to heavenly sons and daughters. Do you understand? "Yes." 

Therefore, when living alone, you must completely settle the path of indemnity. If not, after getting married, Satan will say, "Hey, you still haven't settled your personal matters, and now that you are married, you will be held accountable," and will guard the back door. Think that you will not become such a person. If the husband falls into such a condition, as a wife, you can defend him, saying, "Hey, this is my husband!" You can say, "If we unite in love, in a position higher than Adam and Eve, who absolutely believe in God, then according to principle, it cannot be taken away." 

The love that is formed in the midst of complete unity before God, having settled all indemnity, cannot be separated, can it? Isn't that the principle? What is united in love without conditions cannot be taken away, isn't that the principle? It is principled. Do you understand? 

Therefore, in the family, the couple must strive to overcome any trials, whether they go through tribes, nations, or the world. 

Let us become the subject who liberates God, the object, sons and daughters, and all things. 

That is why you are not doing the work of the church. You are not helping the teacher to fulfill the teacher's orders! Rather, you must understand that you are receiving the benefits of the teacher's proposed conditions. Receiving instructions from the church means you are in debt. You must understand that. Complaining about the church or anyone else because you do not want to go is forbidden. A person who complains cannot transcend the realm of fall. When Adam fell, when God asked, "Oh, it was the Eve you created who caused the fall," they made excuses to each other. 

When you enter the Unification Church, you inevitably enter a position where you can complain, but if you complain, you cannot go to heaven from within the realm of fall. Do you understand? "Yes." 

The same goes for the teacher. God told me to work in America, and I am working, but I am being slandered. The nation opposes me, the church opposes me, and everyone is trying to kill me, doing all sorts of things... How much can I complain? But when I try to do it, I do not owe anything to God. I say, "Even if you do not cooperate, I will do it." But you all say, "Oh, the church does not help, and the teacher does not recognize me, what is this?" 

What will you do? "I will obey." What do you want to do with that obedience? Ultimately, it is to achieve completion. What do you want to achieve with that completion? It is to receive and live in God's love. You want to become a husband with God's love and a wife with God's love. That is how you become a happy person, a holy person on this earth, and can liberate all things. To achieve this restoration of indemnity, to liberate the entire fallen world, it is inevitably necessary to do this. 

Therefore, we are going this way. I will influence God, I will influence my husband, I will influence my sons and daughters, and I will influence all things to become the subject of liberation. That is the wish of the Unification Church. 

Now, if you all make such a determination today, I believe that all your wishes will be fulfilled here. Would you like to live like that? Would you like to move? Would you like to act? "Yes." Raise your hands if you will do that. Thank you! (Applause) *
